Quick Start

Option A: Command Line (Headless)

python -m pip install -r requirements.txt -r requirements-ml.txt -e .
python -c "import torch; assert torch.cuda.is_available(), 'GPU required'"
python -c "
import pandas as pd; from pathlib import Path; import shutil, sys
sys.path.insert(0, 'kronos_repo')
from kth.data.universe import get_all_tickers
from kth.models.kronos_wrapper import KronosTH
from kth.backtest.walkforward import precompute_forecasts

th = KronosTH.from_pretrained('NeoQuasar/Kronos-small', device='cuda')
today = pd.Timestamp.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
slug = 'NeoQuasar_Kronos-small'
today_dir = Path(f'data/forecast_cache/{slug}/{today}')
if today_dir.exists(): shutil.rmtree(today_dir)

precompute_forecasts(th, get_all_tickers(), start_date=today, end_date=today,
                     pred_len=20, n_samples=10, lookback=400)
print(f'Forecasts cached at data/forecast_cache/{slug}/{today}/')
"

Time: GTX 1060 ~12 min | T4 ~3 min | First run +20 min for HF download.

Option B: Notebook (Recommended)

Open notebooks/05_decision_report.ipynb in Jupyter. Set REPORT_MODE = "morning". Run all cells.

⚠️ First run: ~12–15 min (forecast generation). Subsequent runs: ~3 sec (cache hit).

Example Portfolios

Conservative CAGR
5 positions, equal-weight, monthly rebalance. Thai 40% + bonds 20% + cash 40%. 🟢 only.
15–25%
Balanced CAGR
8 positions, inv_vol, monthly. Thai 30% + US 20% + ETF 10% + crypto 5% + cash.

Reading flags: 🟢 = confidence (≤10% uncertainty), not direction. 🟢 on ↓ = confidently bearish.

Cautions & Limitations

This is not financial advice. Forecasts can be wrong. A 60% direction hit-rate means 40% of predictions miss.
  • Survivorship bias: Only currently-listed tickers are in the universe. Delisted stocks are absent — backtests overstate returns.
  • Regime risk: The 2022-2024 period had unique macro conditions (QE unwind, AI boom, SET underperformance). Different regimes produce different results.
  • Crypto calendar mismatch: Backtests use 5-day business calendar; crypto trades 7 days. Sharpe overstated ~20–30% for crypto. Delta between ZS and FT is valid.
  • ETF proxy: ETF class (9 tickers) uses SPY as backtest proxy. Performance on VWO, EWJ, FXI, etc. is untested.
  • 4 untested classes: Commodity, bond_proxy, reit, fx_macro show — in metrics. Do not trade these based solely on model forecasts.
  • Trade win rate 2–5%: This does not mean the model is 95% wrong. It means the portfolio churns positions monthly (11.8× turnover) producing many small losing trades around winning core longs.
  • GPU required: CPU inference is hours vs 15 min on GPU. Use Colab free T4 if you don't have a GPU.

Annual friction drag = Turnover × round-trip friction. Thai: 11.8 × 0.536% = 6.3% of AUM lost to costs annually. CAGR reported is net of these costs.
